<Review>Jorge Cardenas first contacted us in February 2020 asking if we needed maintenance on our HVAC system.  We decided that would be a good idea, and Jorge scheduled a service appointment for us.  As soon as the company's technician walked through the door he realized we had a BIG problem.  Turns out rats had invaded our attic, had chewed holes through the ductwork, and were living INSIDE our HVAC ducting!  AHHHH!!!!! After much discussion with additional company personnel, we settled upon the following services, to be performed as expeditiously as possible: removal of the entire existing HVAC system (i.e., heater, blower, exchanger, exterior A/C unit, ducting, air registers, thermostat; this work began THAT SAME DAY!); removal of all existing attic insulation; rat proofing and sanitizing the attic; installation of an entire new HVAC system (i.e., heater, blower, exchanger, exterior A/C unit, ducting, air registers, thermostat); and installation of new blown in attic insulation. When evidence of rats was discovered after installation of all the new stuff, they sent the rat proofer back to take care of the issue (the initial rat proofing missed the spot where the line from the exterior A/C unit enters the attic). We were VERY relieved that we were no longer breathing rat infused air! And we LOVE our Nest thermostat and the associated Nest app.
Due to the critical nature of the situation (i.e., I wanted those rats out of my ducts NOW!!!), we did not do any comparison shopping to see if we could get a better price with a different company.  Should we have obtained job estimates from other companies? Yes, probably.  But did I want to take the time to do so? NO. GET RID OF THOSE RATS NOW! Did we get a much better HVAC system than we would have purchased under normal circumstances? Definitely!

Here are a few negatives we encountered during this experience:

1. We should have specified that we wanted cellulose rather than fiberglass for the blown-in attic insulation.  Hopefully we will never need to upgrade our ethernet cabling that is currently in the attic and will have no reason to ever enter our attic.
2. Workers often arrived up to 30 minutes EARLIER than our scheduled appointment time.  When you are just waking up or stepping into the shower first thing in the morning it's a bit difficult to answer the door.  Even when I anticipated the workers would likely arrive early, they arrived even earlier than that!
3. While we did feel a bit of an up-sell pressure to purchase a specific A/C unit, it is THE BEST A/C unit we've ever had and it is sure keeping us cool in this hot weather!  Our EPA certified HVAC Technician son was duly impressed with our new system.  We like to joke that it's our "Mercedes Benz" HVAC system (we are typically Honda/Toyota people).
4. I got the impression the Green Sky financing program (i.e., no payments, no interest if paid in full within two years) we took advantage of added approximately 8% to our cost.  Looking back, we probably should have simply raided the cash in our after tax brokerage account (we had sufficient funds to do so); but since I was enamored of using other people's money, I forgot to "do the math" before making our purchase financing decision. *SIGH* Guess breathing all that rat infused air rattled my brain.<//Review>< pictures>

One of the best taco trucks in Santa Ana. You know when the other three or four trucks have empty lines, but this one is always full, the got the good stuff. AL pastor is my favorite and their cabeza is very good too. They give you caramelized onions and have fresh onion, lime, and cilantro too. < review>
My ultimate street taco place is the one in LA but Oaxaca is pretty close. I especially enjoyed their el pastor. I tried few varieties (asada, al pastor, lengua) but al pastor stands out as my favorite choice of meat. I love the fact that they provide plenty of grilled onion on the side. Last time, I tried their al pastor burrito. I asked them to put the grilled onions inside of burrito then they separated at the end. In my car, I had to perform the operation of putting the onions back into the burrito wrap. With limited space and light, the burrito just fall apart. It was still good but I wished they put the onions for me like I asked. : (<//review>

< Review>
These taco truck is quick, delicious and great prices also! I stop by once and awhile at nights.
Even though theres long lines daily they move pretty quickly and once you order they also prepare them super fast. They have like 3 diferent salsa buckets , big onion and cilantro trays, bucket with sliced limes and another tray with sliced raddishes (rabanos).
I personally love the azada tacos best, chicken are great also, al pastor i liked, chorizo thumbs up also.
The rest i didnt really want to try because i dont want to eat lengua, buche, tripas,.etc.
5 stars from me.
5/2/17<//Review>
